Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^4*arctan(a*x)^2

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^4*arctan(a*x)^3

  Leafcounts = 143 6411   0 0

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^3*arctan(a*x)^3

  Integrand        = x^3*arccot(a*x)^2

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^4*arccot(a*x)^3

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x^3*arccot(a*x)^3
